15.\+6.\+3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ab7eb39d17c2b8f040f7918de538300d3}{Build}} 5.\+1.\+0=============================Release notes -\/ N\+Hibernate -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a956344f548ba7529fd443d1bd393940b}{Version}} 5.\+1.\+0 $\ast$$\ast$Highlights $\ast$N\+Hibernate has gained two new target frameworks\+:.\+Net Core 2.\+0 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} .Net Standard 2.\+0. N\+Hibernate Nu\+Get \mbox{\hyperlink{_unity_8_mvc5_81_84_80_2_readme_8txt_a78f0a5e1c91eeee944e60b58f1fdefcd}{package}} provides them, along \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the .Net framework 4.\+6.\+1 build. For \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a14c3a401d863646681a42df2779ef995}{these}} new frameworks, some additional specificities \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} limitations apply\+:$\ast$Binary serialization is not supported -\/ the user shall implement serialization surrogates for System.\+Type, Field\+Info, Property\+Info, Method\+Info, Constructor\+Info, Delegate, etc. $\ast$Sql\+Client, Odbc, Oledb drivers are converted to Reflection\+Based\+Driver to avoid the extra dependencies. $\ast$Call\+Session\+Context uses a static Async\+Local field to mimic the Call\+Context behavior. $\ast$System transactions(transaction scopes) are untested, due to the lack of data providers supporting them. $\ast$114 issues were resolved \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} this release. $\ast$Since Ingres9\+Dialect is now supporting sequences, the enhanced-\/sequence identifier generator will default to using a sequence instead of a table. Revert to previous behavior by using its force\+\_\+table\+\_\+use parameter. $\ast$Some overridable methods of the Dialect base class \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} of Ms\+Sql2000\+Dialect have been obsoleted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} favor of new methods. Dialects implementors need to override the replacing methods if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} were overriding the obsolete ones, which are\+:$\ast$Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint\+End(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by $\ast$Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by $\ast$Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint\+End(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint\+End(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$$\ast$Task $\ast$\#1431 Release 5.\+0.\+1 $\ast$\#1405 Remove unused \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} broken N\+Hibernate.\+Setup WiX project \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ab7eb39d17c2b8f040f7918de538300d3}{Build}} 5.\+0.\+0=============================$\ast$$\ast$Highlights $\ast$IO bound methods have gained an async counterpart. Not intended for parallelism, make sure to await each call before further interacting \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a session \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} its queries. $\ast$Strongly typed D\+ML operation(\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af01bb486a22086824f1b9ecb30611e9a}{insert}}/update/delete) are now available as Linq extensions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} queryables. $\ast$Entities collections can be queried \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} .As\+Queryable() Linq extension without being fully loaded. $\ast$Reference \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a302baafba596d0750c815f5e36a9de4a}{documentation}} has been curated \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} completed, notably \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a Linq section. http\+:$\ast$$\ast$Known B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+I\+NG C\+H\+A\+N\+G\+ES from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{N\+H4.\+1.\+1.\+GA}} to 5.\+0.\+0 N\+Hibernate now targets .Net 4.\+6.\+1. Remotion.\+Linq \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Antlr3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a7b421a4ea8b5fcd57b66a885f56c1aa4}{libraries}} are no more merged \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a35643e6cde36e0e5b6d5516664e8c947}{library}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} must be deployed along N\+Hibernate library.(Nu\+Get will reference them.) Classes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} members which were flagged as obsolete \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the N\+Hibernate 4.x series have been dropped. Prior to upgrading, fix any obsolete warning according to its message. See NH-\/4075 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} NH-\/3684 for a list. $\ast$All members exposing some System.\+Data types have been changed for the corresponding System.\+Data.\+Common types.(I\+Db\+Command=$>$ Db\+Command,...) $\ast$The Date N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} will no more replace by null values below its base value(which was year 1753). Its base value is now Date\+Time.\+Min\+Value. Its configuration parameter is obsolete. $\ast$N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} Date\+Time\+Type, which is the default for a .Net Date\+Time, does no longer cut fractional seconds. Use Date\+Time\+No\+Ms\+Type if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} wish to have fractional seconds cut. It applies to its Local/Utc counterparts too. $\ast$Local\+Date\+Time\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Utc\+Date\+Time\+Type do no more accept being set \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a value having a non-\/matching kind, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} throw instead. $\ast$Db\+Timestamp will now round the retrieved value according to Dialect.\+Timestamp\+Resolution\+In\+Ticks. $\ast$When an object typed property is mapped to a N\+Hibernate timestamp, setting an invalid object \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the property will now throw at flush instead of replacing \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} Date\+Time.\+Now. $\ast$Decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration now correctly handles maximal precision. For most dialects, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} is 28, matching the .Net limit. Values \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} mappings \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aadd2157482c040487672f890e730bb09}{above}} maximal precision will be reduced to maximal precision. $\ast$Default cast types do no more resolve string to 255 length \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} decimal to its default precision/scale for the dialect. They resolve to 4000 length string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}}(28, 10) precision/scale decimals by default, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} are trimmed down according to dialect. Those defaults can be overridden \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+length, query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+scale settings. $\ast$Future queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} data provider not actually supporting them(not supporting mutliple queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} a single S\+QL command) are no more immediately executed at the .Future call. They are executed only when directly enumerated \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} when their I\+Future\+Enumerable.\+Get\+Enumerable \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} is called.(This aligns them \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the behavior of Future\+Value.) $\ast$Dialects are now configurable. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a639f8d73f895ba1d65ad9df8173ea738}{If}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} instantiate a dialect directly, make sure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} call its Configure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} as argument the properties of a N\+Hibernate Configuration object. You may \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} instead Dialect.\+Get\+Dialect methods, which configure the dialect before returning it. $\ast$Transaction scopes handling has undergone a major rework. See NH-\/4011 for full details. $\ast$$\ast$More transaction promotion to \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0b0015f76c0b6dfe70b6fd8b7a3b645f}{distributed}} may occur if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} the \char`\"{}flush \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} commit\char`\"{} feature \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} transaction scopes. Explicitly flush your session instead. Ensure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} does not occur by disabling transaction.\+use\+\_\+connection\+\_\+on\+\_\+system\+\_\+prepare setting. $\ast$$\ast$After transaction events no more allow using the connection when \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} are raised from a scope completion. $\ast$$\ast$Connection enlistment \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} an ambient transaction is now enforced by N\+Hibernate by default. $\ast$$\ast$The connection \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a285084160888c7c78264cdce3f915c4b}{releasing}} is no more directly triggered by a scope completion, but by later interactions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the session. $\ast$Ado\+Net\+With\+Distributed\+Transaction\+Factory has been renamed Ado\+Net\+With\+System\+Transaction\+Factory. $\ast$Subcriteria.\+Unique\+Result$<$ T $>$ for value types now return default(T) when result is null, as was already doing Criteria\+Impl.\+Unique\+Result$<$ T $>$. $\ast$Alias\+To\+Bean\+Result\+Transformer property/field resolution logic has changed for supporting members which names differ only by case. See NH-\/3693 last comments for details. $\ast$Linq inequality implementation has been changed for supporting null, meaning \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} a \char`\"{}a != b\char`\"{} expression will now be considered matching if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a6a2b11d0e95bd2a3022eb2d52a00baf0}{one}} side is null, while previously due to S\+QL null semantic \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} was considered non-\/matching. See NH-\/3100. $\ast$Linq extension methods marked \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} attribute Linq\+Extension\+Method will no more be evaluated \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}}-\/memory prior to query execution when \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} do not depend \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} query \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a255314fbf618cad02318ed584c41b8d2}{results}}, but will always be translated to their corresponding S\+QL call. This can be changed \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a parameter of the attribute. $\ast$Linq Query methods are now native members of I\+Session \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+Stateless\+Session instead of being extension methods. $\ast$Linq provider now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} Remotion.\+Linq v2, which may break Linq provider extensions, mainly due to names changes. See https\+:$\ast$N\+Hibernate Linq internals have undergone some minor changes which may break custom Linq providers due to \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} signature changes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} additional methods to implement. $\ast$I\+Mapping interface has an additional Dialect member. I\+Session\+Factory\+Implementor has lost \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}}, since \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} gains \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} back through I\+Mapping. $\ast$I\+Driver.\+Expand\+Query\+Parameters \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Driver\+Base.\+Clone\+Parameter take an additional argument. $\ast$Nullable\+Type, its descendent(notably all Primitive\+Type) \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+User\+Type value getters \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} setters now take the session as an argument. This should mainly impact custom types implementors. $\ast$Emit\+Util is now internal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} has been cleaned of unused members. $\ast$Contraint\+Ordered\+Table\+Key\+Column\+Closure has been renamed Constraint\+Ordered\+Table\+Key\+Column\+Closure. $\ast$enabled\+Filter parameter has been removed from I\+Projection.\+To\+Sql\+String \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+Criterion.\+To\+Sql\+String methods. $\ast$Proxy factory \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} proxy cache now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} Type\+Info instead of System.\+Type. This should be transparent for most users. $\ast$Exceptions which were based \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} Application\+Exception are now based \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} Exception\+:\+Hibernate\+Exception, Parser\+Exception \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Assertion\+Failure. The logger factory which could throw a bare Application\+Exception now throws an Instantiation\+Exception instead. $\ast$Thread\+Safe\+Dictionary class has been removed. Use System.\+Collections.\+Concurrent.\+Concurrent\+Dictionary instead. $\ast$Entity mode switching capability, which had never been fully implemented, is dropped. $\ast$Bytecode\+Provider\+Impl, intended for .Net Framework 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} broken, is dropped. $\ast$Sessions concrete classes constructors have been changed.(It is not expected for them to be used directly.) $\ast$Obsolete setting interceptors.\+beforetransactioncompletion\+\_\+ignore\+\_\+exceptions is dropped. $\ast$S\+QL Server 2008+dialects now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} datetime2 instead of datetime for all date-\/time types, including timestamp. This can be reverted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} sql\+\_\+types.\+keep\+\_\+datetime setting. $\ast$S\+QL Server 2008+timestamp resolution is now 100ns \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} accordance \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} datetime2 capabilities, down from 10ms previously. This can be reverted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} sql\+\_\+types.\+keep\+\_\+datetime setting. $\ast$Oracle 9g+dialects now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} timestamp(7) for all date time types, instead of timestamp(4). $\ast$Oracle 9g+timestamp resolution is now 100ns \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} accordance \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} timestamp(7) capabilities, down from 100µs previously. $\ast$Oracle\+:\+Hbm2dll will no-\/more choose N-\/ prefixed types for typing Unicode string columns by default. This can be changed \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} oracle.\+use\+\_\+n\+\_\+prefixed\+\_\+types\+\_\+for\+\_\+unicode setting, which will furthermore control Db\+Command \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a4ff3b40dd630814cc9ceb2f3b05f6f52}{parameters}} typing accordingly. See NH-\/4062. $\ast$Sql\+Server\+Ce\+:the id generator \char`\"{}native\char`\"{} will now resolve as \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}-\/hilo instead of identity. $\ast$Firebird\+:timestamp resolution is now 1ms. $\ast$Postgre\+S\+Q\+L\+:if Npgsql v3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} later is used, time Db\+Parameters will be fetched as Time\+Span instead of Date\+Time. $\ast$D\+B2 \&Oracle lite\+:decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration was hardcoding precision as 19 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} was using length as scale. It now uses precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} scale from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}} when specified, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} disregards length. $\ast$Ingres \&Sybase A\+S\+A\+:decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration was hardcoding precision as 18 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} was using length as scale. It now uses precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} scale from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}} when specified, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} disregards length. $\ast$O\+D\+B\+C\+:\+String parameter length will no more be specified by the Odbc\+Driver. 4.\+1.\+0.\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{GA}}=============================Proxies for classes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} used \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aa7e0b385aad3ecc67e334144a66cdf05}{lazy}} fields(not collections) would have any exceptions from the entity wrapped \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Target\+Invocation\+Exception. This wrapping \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} have now been removed. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a1d7ad03014b6bcf1bf8ced186e60f1fc}{Where}} relevant, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} should instead catch the original \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} throw. For L\+I\+NQ queries, the start\+At parameter \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} the return value for string.\+Index\+Of() are now correctly translated from .Net \textquotesingle{}s 0-\/based indexing to S\+QL \textquotesingle{}s 1-\/based indexing. L\+I\+NQ queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} are written to expect S\+QL semantics for Index\+Of() will likely need to be adjusted(NH-\/3846, NH-\/3901). Example\+:A L\+I\+NQ query should now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} \textquotesingle{}x=$>$x.\+Name.\+Index\+Of(\char`\"{}a\char`\"{})==-\/1\textquotesingle{} to pick objects where the name doesn \textquotesingle{}t contain the letter \char`\"{}a\char`\"{}. This change will primarily affect loading of \mbox{\hyperlink{_unity_8_mvc5_81_84_80_2_readme_8txt_a36bd0c16c72dd791d4039e75c4bd479a}{A\+D\+O.\+N\+ET}} data provider assemblies. 0.\+99.\+1.\+0 (1.\+0-\/rc1) ======================== Breaking changes to external A\+P\+I\+: -\/ Updated to a newer \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} of Castle.\+Dynamic\+Proxy. W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+G\+: this new \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} has the same \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a839cee5f06e0d8ce20519eec62121b15}{number}} (1.\+1.\+5.\+0) as the \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} used by the previous release of N\+Hibernate, but the binaries are \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} fact different \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} the old 1.\+1.\+5.\+0 will not \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a1b5470c60688358a70a69f8556894407}{work}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} 1.\+0-\/rc1. -\/ N\+Hibernate no longer configures log4net internally. It is now up to the user to configure logging. -\/ Accessing a disposed \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} closed I\+Session \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} I\+Transaction now causes an Object\+Disposed\+Exception. Hibernate\+Exception \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} Transaction\+Exception could be thrown \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} this \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ac25546546ad3dde8a40a9c987d5d1adc}{case}} before, such cases were also changed to throw Object\+Disposed\+Exception. -\/ Renamed S\+Q\+L\+Expression to S\+Q\+L\+Criterion per Hibernate 2.\+1. Now, \{alias\} should be used instead of \$alias \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} S\+QL criteria. -\/ Unused constructors for some exceptions were removed. Breaking changes to N\+Hibernate extension interfaces\+: -\/ Renamed I\+Class\+Persister.\+Is\+Default\+Version to Is\+Unsaved\+Version. It now takes as argument an array of property values instead of an object. -\/ Renamed I\+Class\+Persister.\+Current\+Version to Get\+Current\+Version to follow naming conventions closer. -\/ Fixed Match\+Mode.\+Start \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Match\+Mode.\+End for Like expressions, their meanings were reversed. -\/ Dialect.\+Add\+Identity\+Select\+To\+Insert should now return null if the functionality is not supported, instead of throwing an exception. Bug fixes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} enhancements\+: -\/ Ported almost all remaining Hibernate 2.\+1 features to N\+Hibernate\+: $\ast$ subcriteria $\ast$ meta attributes $\ast$ optimistic-\/lock setting $\ast$ query cache $\ast$ select-\/before-\/update $\ast$ batch \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aa7e0b385aad3ecc67e334144a66cdf05}{lazy}} loading $\ast$ dynamic components Missing features are Databinder, Scrollable\+Results \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Schema\+Update. -\/ Allow serializing an unflushed session (NH-\/292, Yves Dierick). -\/ Check \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} composite id classes override Get\+Hash\+Code \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Equals. -\/ Throw Query\+Exception when attempting to fetch multiple collections \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} a query. -\/ Added a Section\+Handler to allow using .cfg.\+xml syntax to configure N\+Hibernate from App.\+config files. (This was already part of 0.\+9.\+1 release but was not announced \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the release notes.) -\/ Fixed bug when using joined-\/subclass \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} key-\/many-\/to-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a6a2b11d0e95bd2a3022eb2d52a00baf0}{one}} (NH-\/369). -\/ Added I\+Type implementations \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} constants \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} N\+Hibernate\+Util for unsigned integer types. -\/ Added index attribute for $<$property$>$. -\/ Schema\+Export now generates S\+QL to create an index when index attribute is used \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} $<$property$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} $<$column$>$. -\/ Schema\+Export will add an \char`\"{}if exists\char`\"{} clause to \char`\"{}drop \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}\char`\"{} statement, if supported by the dialect. -\/ Heavy refactoring of the \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a302baafba596d0750c815f5e36a9de4a}{documentation}}

Change by setting default-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aa7e0b385aad3ecc67e334144a66cdf05}{lazy}}=\char`\"{}false\char`\"{} in $<$hibernate-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}}$>$. $\ast$ Types used as proxies are now validated (a check is done \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} all public members are virtual). Validation can be disabled by setting hibernate.\+use\+\_\+proxy\+\_\+validator to false. $\ast$ I\+Session.\+Get/Load now obey where=\char`\"{}...\char`\"{} attribute of $<$class$>$. $\ast$ Assemblies are signed using a new, publicly available, key. $\ast$ Assembly.\+Load\+With\+Partial\+Name is no longer used to load assemblies. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a639f8d73f895ba1d65ad9df8173ea738}{If}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} want NH to load an assembly from the G\+AC, \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} $<$qualify\+Assembly$>$ element \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the configuration file to specify its fully qualified name. This change will primarily affect loading of \mbox{\hyperlink{_unity_8_mvc5_81_84_80_2_readme_8txt_a36bd0c16c72dd791d4039e75c4bd479a}{A\+D\+O.\+N\+ET}} data provider assemblies. $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/398\mbox{]} -\/ Bulk property get/set optimization \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Abstract\+Entity\+Persister contributed by Roberto Paterlini. The optimization is enabled by default, set hibernate.\+use\+\_\+reflection\+\_\+optimizer property to false \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} your App.\+config file to disable it. Note \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} the property is global, thus \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} is only possible to set \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the app.\+config file \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} $<$nhibernate$>$ session (see \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aadd2157482c040487672f890e730bb09}{above}}). $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/443\mbox{]} -\/ Added more details to \char`\"{}broken column \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}}\char`\"{} message $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/448\mbox{]} -\/ N\+Hibernate configuration process is now closer to Hibernate\+: -\/ hibernate.\+properties file corresponds to $<$nhibernate$>$ section \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} app.\+config (mapped to Name\+Value\+Section\+Handler) -\/ configuration through hibernate.\+cfg.\+xml is supported -\/ instead of hibernate.\+cfg.\+xml, $<$hibernate-\/configuration$>$ section \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} app.\+config (mapped to N\+Hibernate.\+Cfg.\+Configuration\+Section\+Handler) can also be used. -\/ creating a new configuration instance \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} 1.\+0 would cause \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} to read $<$hibernate-\/configuration$>$ section immediately. In 1.\+0.\+1 this was changed \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a992e0bb184d6325b80f65d6bedfaa160}{so}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} the section is only read when Configure() is called $\ast$ Hash\+Code\+Provider is now merged into N\+Hibernate assembly during build, thus \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} does not have to be \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0b0015f76c0b6dfe70b6fd8b7a3b645f}{distributed}} along \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} N\+Hibernate.\+dll. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ab7eb39d17c2b8f040f7918de538300d3}{Build}} 1.\+0.\+0.\+0 ======================== Improvements\+: $\ast$ I\+Transaction.\+Commit \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Rollback will not wrap exceptions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} derive from Hibernate\+Exception into Transaction\+Exceptions, those exceptions will instead be propagated untouched. $\ast$ Field\+Accessor now includes correct \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Property\+Not\+Found\+Exception. $\ast$ Oracle9\+Dialect will now generate a column of \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+MP(4) for date fields mapped as \char`\"{}datetime\char`\"{}. Build 0.\+99.\+3.\+0 (1.\+0-\/rc3) ======================== Bug Fixes\+: $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/376\mbox{]} -\/ Expression.\+In w/ an empty collection causes a S\+QL \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/382, NH-\/392\mbox{]} -\/ problems \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} A\+DO transactions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} plagued previous 1.\+0-\/rcX versions should all be resolved now. $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/391\mbox{]} -\/ Bug \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Read\+Write\+Cache when session is opened \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} existing connection $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/394\mbox{]} -\/ Null\+Reference\+Exception \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} debug print of session objects. $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/396\mbox{]} -\/ User-\/provided class names should be trimmed before \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/397\mbox{]} -\/ Configuration\+Section\+Handler doesn\textquotesingle{}t reads empty properties Improvements\+: $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/388\mbox{]} -\/ Support for the \char`\"{}Any\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}Meta-\/Value\char`\"{} tags $\ast$ Added fetch attribute from Hibernate 3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} values \char`\"{}select\char`\"{}/\char`\"{}join\char`\"{}. fetch=\char`\"{}select\char`\"{} is equivalent to outer-\/join=\char`\"{}false\char`\"{}, and fetch=\char`\"{}join\char`\"{} matches outer-\/join=\char`\"{}true\char`\"{}. 0.\+99.\+1.\+0 (1.\+0-\/rc1) ======================== Breaking changes to external A\+P\+I\+: -\/ Updated to a newer \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} of Castle.\+Dynamic\+Proxy. W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+G\+: this new \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} has the same \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a839cee5f06e0d8ce20519eec62121b15}{number}} (1.\+1.\+5.\+0) as the \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} used by the previous release of N\+Hibernate, but the binaries are \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} fact different \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} the old 1.\+1.\+5.\+0 will not \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a1b5470c60688358a70a69f8556894407}{work}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} 1.\+0-\/rc1. -\/ N\+Hibernate no longer configures log4net internally. It is now up to the user to configure logging. -\/ Accessing a disposed \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} closed I\+Session \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} I\+Transaction now causes an Object\+Disposed\+Exception. Hibernate\+Exception \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} Transaction\+Exception could be thrown \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} this \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ac25546546ad3dde8a40a9c987d5d1adc}{case}} before, such cases were also changed to throw Object\+Disposed\+Exception. -\/ Renamed S\+Q\+L\+Expression to S\+Q\+L\+Criterion per Hibernate 2.\+1. Now, \{alias\} should be used instead of \$alias \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} S\+QL criteria. -\/ Unused constructors for some exceptions were removed. Breaking changes to N\+Hibernate extension interfaces\+: -\/ Renamed I\+Class\+Persister.\+Is\+Default\+Version to Is\+Unsaved\+Version. It now takes as argument an array of property values instead of an object. -\/ Renamed I\+Class\+Persister.\+Current\+Version to Get\+Current\+Version to follow naming conventions closer. -\/ Fixed Match\+Mode.\+Start \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Match\+Mode.\+End for Like expressions, their meanings were reversed. -\/ Dialect.\+Add\+Identity\+Select\+To\+Insert should now return null if the functionality is not supported, instead of throwing an exception. Bug fixes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} enhancements\+: -\/ Ported almost all remaining Hibernate 2.\+1 features to N\+Hibernate\+: $\ast$ subcriteria $\ast$ meta attributes $\ast$ optimistic-\/lock setting $\ast$ query cache $\ast$ select-\/before-\/update $\ast$ batch \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aa7e0b385aad3ecc67e334144a66cdf05}{lazy}} loading $\ast$ dynamic components Missing features are Databinder, Scrollable\+Results \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Schema\+Update. -\/ Allow serializing an unflushed session (NH-\/292, Yves Dierick). -\/ Check \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} composite id classes override Get\+Hash\+Code \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Equals. -\/ Throw Query\+Exception when attempting to fetch multiple collections \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} a query. -\/ Added a Section\+Handler to allow using .cfg.\+xml syntax to configure N\+Hibernate from App.\+config files. (This was already part of 0.\+9.\+1 release but was not announced \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the release notes.) -\/ Fixed bug when using joined-\/subclass \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} key-\/many-\/to-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a6a2b11d0e95bd2a3022eb2d52a00baf0}{one}} (NH-\/369). -\/ Added I\+Type implementations \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} constants \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} N\+Hibernate\+Util for unsigned integer types. -\/ Added index attribute for $<$property$>$. -\/ Schema\+Export now generates S\+QL to create an index when index attribute is used \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} $<$property$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} $<$column$>$. -\/ Schema\+Export will add an \char`\"{}if exists\char`\"{} clause to \char`\"{}drop \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}\char`\"{} statement, if supported by the dialect. -\/ Heavy refactoring of the \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a302baafba596d0750c815f5e36a9de4a}{documentation}}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a956344f548ba7529fd443d1bd393940b}{Version}} 5.\+1.\+0 $\ast$$\ast$ Highlights $\ast$ N\+Hibernate has gained two new target frameworks\+: .Net Core 2.\+0 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} .Net Standard 2.\+0. N\+Hibernate Nu\+Get \mbox{\hyperlink{_unity_8_mvc5_81_84_80_2_readme_8txt_a78f0a5e1c91eeee944e60b58f1fdefcd}{package}} provides them, along \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the .Net framework 4.\+6.\+1 build. For \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a14c3a401d863646681a42df2779ef995}{these}} new frameworks, some additional specificities \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} limitations apply\+: $\ast$ Binary serialization is not supported -\/ the user shall implement serialization surrogates for System.\+Type, Field\+Info, Property\+Info, Method\+Info, Constructor\+Info, Delegate, etc. $\ast$ Sql\+Client, Odbc, Oledb drivers are converted to Reflection\+Based\+Driver to avoid the extra dependencies. $\ast$ Call\+Session\+Context uses a static Async\+Local field to mimic the Call\+Context behavior. $\ast$ System transactions (transaction scopes) are untested, due to the lack of data providers supporting them. $\ast$ 114 issues were resolved \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} this release. $\ast$ Since Ingres9\+Dialect is now supporting sequences, the enhanced-\/sequence identifier generator will default to using a sequence instead of a table. Revert to previous behavior by using its force\+\_\+table\+\_\+use parameter. $\ast$ Some overridable methods of the Dialect base class \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} of Ms\+Sql2000\+Dialect have been obsoleted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} favor of new methods. Dialects implementors need to override the replacing methods if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} were overriding the obsolete ones, which are\+: $\ast$ Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$ Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint\+End(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Not\+Exists\+Create\+Constraint\+End(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$ Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$ Dialect.\+Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint\+End(Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name), replaced by Get\+If\+Exists\+Drop\+Constraint\+End(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$ Ms\+Sql2000\+Dialect.\+Get\+Select\+Existing\+Object(string name, Table \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}), replaced by Get\+Select\+Existing\+Object(string catalog, string schema, string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}, string name). $\ast$$\ast$ Bug $\ast$ \#1606 N\+Hibernate 5 precision maximum \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} decimal reduced vs. N\+Hibernate 4 $\ast$ \#1605 My\+Sql batcher may attempt initiating a new batch without closing open reader first. $\ast$ \#1604 My\+Sql batcher disables db \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} $\ast$$\ast$ Task $\ast$ \#1431 Release 5.\+0.\+1 $\ast$ \#1405 Remove unused \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} broken N\+Hibernate.\+Setup WiX project \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ab7eb39d17c2b8f040f7918de538300d3}{Build}} 5.\+0.\+0 ============================= $\ast$$\ast$ Highlights $\ast$ IO bound methods have gained an async counterpart. Not intended for parallelism, make sure to await each call before further interacting \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a session \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} its queries. $\ast$ Strongly typed D\+ML operation (\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af01bb486a22086824f1b9ecb30611e9a}{insert}}/update/delete) are now available as Linq extensions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} queryables. $\ast$ Entities collections can be queried \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} .As\+Queryable() Linq extension without being fully loaded. $\ast$ Reference \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a302baafba596d0750c815f5e36a9de4a}{documentation}} has been curated \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} completed, notably \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a Linq section. http\+: $\ast$$\ast$ Known B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+I\+NG C\+H\+A\+N\+G\+ES from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{N\+H4.\+1.\+1.\+GA}} to 5.\+0.\+0 N\+Hibernate now targets .Net 4.\+6.\+1. Remotion.\+Linq \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Antlr3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a7b421a4ea8b5fcd57b66a885f56c1aa4}{libraries}} are no more merged \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a35643e6cde36e0e5b6d5516664e8c947}{library}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} must be deployed along N\+Hibernate library. (Nu\+Get will reference them.) Classes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} members which were flagged as obsolete \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the N\+Hibernate 4.x series have been dropped. Prior to upgrading, fix any obsolete warning according to its message. See NH-\/4075 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} NH-\/3684 for a list. $\ast$ All members exposing some System.\+Data types have been changed for the corresponding System.\+Data.\+Common types. (I\+Db\+Command =$>$ Db\+Command, ...) $\ast$ The Date N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} will no more replace by null values below its base value (which was year 1753). Its base value is now Date\+Time.\+Min\+Value. Its configuration parameter is obsolete. $\ast$ N\+Hibernate \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} Date\+Time\+Type, which is the default for a .Net Date\+Time, does no longer cut fractional seconds. Use Date\+Time\+No\+Ms\+Type if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} wish to have fractional seconds cut. It applies to its Local/Utc counterparts too. $\ast$ Local\+Date\+Time\+Type \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Utc\+Date\+Time\+Type do no more accept being set \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a value having a non-\/matching kind, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} throw instead. $\ast$ Db\+Timestamp will now round the retrieved value according to Dialect.\+Timestamp\+Resolution\+In\+Ticks. $\ast$ When an object typed property is mapped to a N\+Hibernate timestamp, setting an invalid object \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the property will now throw at flush instead of replacing \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} Date\+Time.\+Now. $\ast$ Decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration now correctly handles maximal precision. For most dialects, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} is 28, matching the .Net limit. Values \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} mappings \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aadd2157482c040487672f890e730bb09}{above}} maximal precision will be reduced to maximal precision. $\ast$ Default cast types do no more resolve string to 255 length \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} decimal to its default precision/scale for the dialect. They resolve to 4000 length string \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} (28, 10) precision/scale decimals by default, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} are trimmed down according to dialect. Those defaults can be overridden \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+length, query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} query.\+default\+\_\+cast\+\_\+scale settings. $\ast$ Future queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} data provider not actually supporting them (not supporting mutliple queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} a single S\+QL command) are no more immediately executed at the .Future call. They are executed only when directly enumerated \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} when their I\+Future\+Enumerable.\+Get\+Enumerable \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} is called. (This aligns them \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the behavior of Future\+Value.) $\ast$ Dialects are now configurable. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a639f8d73f895ba1d65ad9df8173ea738}{If}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} instantiate a dialect directly, make sure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} call its Configure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} as argument the properties of a N\+Hibernate Configuration object. You may \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} instead Dialect.\+Get\+Dialect methods, which configure the dialect before returning it. $\ast$ Transaction scopes handling has undergone a major rework. See NH-\/4011 for full details. $\ast$$\ast$ More transaction promotion to \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0b0015f76c0b6dfe70b6fd8b7a3b645f}{distributed}} may occur if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} the \char`\"{}flush \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} commit\char`\"{} feature \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} transaction scopes. Explicitly flush your session instead. Ensure \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} does not occur by disabling transaction.\+use\+\_\+connection\+\_\+on\+\_\+system\+\_\+prepare setting. $\ast$$\ast$ After transaction events no more allow using the connection when \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} are raised from a scope completion. $\ast$$\ast$ Connection enlistment \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} an ambient transaction is now enforced by N\+Hibernate by default. $\ast$$\ast$ The connection \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a285084160888c7c78264cdce3f915c4b}{releasing}} is no more directly triggered by a scope completion, but by later interactions \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} the session. $\ast$ Ado\+Net\+With\+Distributed\+Transaction\+Factory has been renamed Ado\+Net\+With\+System\+Transaction\+Factory. $\ast$ Subcriteria.\+Unique\+Result$<$T$>$ for value types now return default(T) when result is null, as was already doing Criteria\+Impl.\+Unique\+Result$<$T$>$. $\ast$ Alias\+To\+Bean\+Result\+Transformer property/field resolution logic has changed for supporting members which names differ only by case. See NH-\/3693 last comments for details. $\ast$ Linq inequality implementation has been changed for supporting null, meaning \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} a \char`\"{}a != b\char`\"{} expression will now be considered matching if \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a6a2b11d0e95bd2a3022eb2d52a00baf0}{one}} side is null, while previously due to S\+QL null semantic \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} was considered non-\/matching. See NH-\/3100. $\ast$ Linq extension methods marked \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} attribute Linq\+Extension\+Method will no more be evaluated \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}}-\/memory prior to query execution when \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad13dd895315182151260cab9a07dae0e}{they}} do not depend \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} query \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a255314fbf618cad02318ed584c41b8d2}{results}}, but will always be translated to their corresponding S\+QL call. This can be changed \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a parameter of the attribute. $\ast$ Linq Query methods are now native members of I\+Session \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+Stateless\+Session instead of being extension methods. $\ast$ Linq provider now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} Remotion.\+Linq v2, which may break Linq provider extensions, mainly due to names changes. See https\+: $\ast$ N\+Hibernate Linq internals have undergone some minor changes which may break custom Linq providers due to \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} signature changes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} additional methods to implement. $\ast$ I\+Mapping interface has an additional Dialect member. I\+Session\+Factory\+Implementor has lost \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}}, since \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} gains \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} back through I\+Mapping. $\ast$ I\+Driver.\+Expand\+Query\+Parameters \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Driver\+Base.\+Clone\+Parameter take an additional argument. $\ast$ Nullable\+Type, its descendent (notably all Primitive\+Type) \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+User\+Type value getters \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} setters now take the session as an argument. This should mainly impact custom types implementors. $\ast$ Emit\+Util is now internal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} has been cleaned of unused members. $\ast$ Contraint\+Ordered\+Table\+Key\+Column\+Closure has been renamed Constraint\+Ordered\+Table\+Key\+Column\+Closure. $\ast$ enabled\+Filter parameter has been removed from I\+Projection.\+To\+Sql\+String \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} I\+Criterion.\+To\+Sql\+String methods. $\ast$ Proxy factory \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} proxy cache now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} Type\+Info instead of System.\+Type. This should be transparent for most users. $\ast$ Exceptions which were based \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} Application\+Exception are now based \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} Exception\+: Hibernate\+Exception, Parser\+Exception \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Assertion\+Failure. The logger factory which could throw a bare Application\+Exception now throws an Instantiation\+Exception instead. $\ast$ Thread\+Safe\+Dictionary class has been removed. Use System.\+Collections.\+Concurrent.\+Concurrent\+Dictionary instead. $\ast$ Entity mode switching capability, which had never been fully implemented, is dropped. $\ast$ Bytecode\+Provider\+Impl, intended for .Net Framework 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} broken, is dropped. $\ast$ Sessions concrete classes constructors have been changed. (It is not expected for them to be used directly.) $\ast$ Obsolete setting interceptors.\+beforetransactioncompletion\+\_\+ignore\+\_\+exceptions is dropped. $\ast$ S\+QL Server 2008+ dialects now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} datetime2 instead of datetime for all date-\/time types, including timestamp. This can be reverted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} sql\+\_\+types.\+keep\+\_\+datetime setting. $\ast$ S\+QL Server 2008+ timestamp resolution is now 100ns \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} accordance \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} datetime2 capabilities, down from 10ms previously. This can be reverted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} sql\+\_\+types.\+keep\+\_\+datetime setting. $\ast$ Oracle 9g+ dialects now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} timestamp(7) for all date time types, instead of timestamp(4). $\ast$ Oracle 9g+ timestamp resolution is now 100ns \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} accordance \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} timestamp(7) capabilities, down from 100µs previously. $\ast$ Oracle\+: Hbm2dll will no-\/more choose N-\/ prefixed types for typing Unicode string columns by default. This can be changed \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} oracle.\+use\+\_\+n\+\_\+prefixed\+\_\+types\+\_\+for\+\_\+unicode setting, which will furthermore control Db\+Command \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a4ff3b40dd630814cc9ceb2f3b05f6f52}{parameters}} typing accordingly. See NH-\/4062. $\ast$ Sql\+Server\+Ce\+: the id generator \char`\"{}native\char`\"{} will now resolve as \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}}-\/hilo instead of identity. $\ast$ Firebird\+: timestamp resolution is now 1ms. $\ast$ Postgre\+S\+Q\+L\+: if Npgsql v3 \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} later is used, time Db\+Parameters will be fetched as Time\+Span instead of Date\+Time. $\ast$ D\+B2 \& Oracle lite\+: decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration was hardcoding precision as 19 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} was using length as scale. It now uses precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} scale from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}} when specified, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} disregards length. $\ast$ Ingres \& Sybase A\+S\+A\+: decimal \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} registration was hardcoding precision as 18 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} was using length as scale. It now uses precision \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} scale from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}} when specified, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} disregards length. $\ast$ O\+D\+B\+C\+: String parameter length will no more be specified by the Odbc\+Driver. 4.\+1.\+1.\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{GA}} ============================= The \mbox{[}NH-\/3904\mbox{]} has been reverted \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a4ff3b40dd630814cc9ceb2f3b05f6f52}{parameters}} $\ast$$\ast$ Bug $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/3929\mbox{]} -\/ Expression\+Parameter\+Visitor selects wrong Custom\+Type for Constant\+Expression (Linq) $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/3941\mbox{]} -\/ Mapped\+As() does 4.\+1.\+0.\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{GA}} ============================= Proxies for classes \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} used \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aa7e0b385aad3ecc67e334144a66cdf05}{lazy}} fields (not collections) would have any exceptions from the entity wrapped \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Target\+Invocation\+Exception. This wrapping \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} have now been removed. \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a1d7ad03014b6bcf1bf8ced186e60f1fc}{Where}} relevant, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} should instead catch the original \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_ad8404db5e23841dcb367ab565ba9dfd6}{exception}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a56883a24ef59d90cb22e5085c7bf29e3}{type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_aa3e27662c1d4cbafd95f10f5d4c51aed}{you}} throw. For L\+I\+NQ queries, the start\+At parameter \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} the return value for string.\+Index\+Of() are now correctly translated from .Net\textquotesingle{}s 0-\/based indexing to S\+QL\textquotesingle{}s 1-\/based indexing. L\+I\+NQ queries \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} are written to expect S\+QL semantics for Index\+Of() will likely need to be adjusted (NH-\/3846, NH-\/3901). Example\+: A L\+I\+NQ query should now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} \textquotesingle{}x=$>$x.\+Name.\+Index\+Of(\char`\"{}a\char`\"{}) == -\/1\textquotesingle{} to pick objects where the name doesn\textquotesingle{}t contain the letter \char`\"{}a\char`\"{}. $\ast$$\ast$ Bug $\ast$ \mbox{[}NH-\/3885\mbox{]} -\/ Thread\+Safe\+Dictionary is not threadsafe \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ab7eb39d17c2b8f040f7918de538300d3}{Build}} ============================= $\ast$$\ast$ Known B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+I\+NG C\+H\+A\+N\+G\+ES from \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{N\+H3.\+3.\+3.\+GA}} to 4.\+0.\+0.\mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_aee430ddae3df9b208a12004094c0cf1b}{GA}} N\+Hibernate now targets .Net 4.\+0. Many uses of set types from Iesi.\+Collections have now been changed to \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} corresponding types from the B\+C\+L. The A\+PI for \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a14c3a401d863646681a42df2779ef995}{these}} types are slightly different. Support for persistent non-\/generic collections removed. Use the generic counterparts instead. $\ast$ I\+Delete\+Event\+Listener, I\+Event\+Source\+: Use generic I\+Set$<$$>$ instead of non-\/generic \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} signatures. $\ast$ Sql\+String.\+Parts removed. Use Sql\+String.\+Count \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Sql\+String.\+Get\+Enumerator(). $\ast$ I\+Persistent\+Collection.\+Get\+Snapshot() now returns object instead of I\+Collection. The snapshot should be opaque to outside code. $\ast$ Removed Is\+Discriminator\+Formula, Discriminator\+Formula \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Generate\+Select\+String from Union\+Subclass\+Entity\+Persister class. $\ast$ Removed Managed\+Web\+Session\+Context. Any configuration \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a7ed69f4f60811a370abadce81b6ddd2c}{files}} which \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} the \char`\"{}managed\+\_\+web\char`\"{} session context should now \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_abc7f7a8be919ef8b5d01a8af31c2b39f}{use}} \char`\"{}web\char`\"{} $\ast$ Sybase\+A\+S\+A\+Dialect removed\+: Use Sybase\+S\+Q\+L\+Anywhere10\+Dialect instead. $\ast$ A\+S\+A10\+Client\+Driver, A\+S\+A\+Client\+Driver \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} S\+Q\+Lite\+Driver removed\+: Use Sybase\+S\+Q\+L\+Anywhere\+Driver, Sybase\+Asa\+Client\+Driver, S\+Q\+Lite20\+Driver instead. $\ast$ Removed Classic H\+QL Parser. $\ast$ Removed I\+Query\+Translator\+Factory2. It\textquotesingle{}s methods were pulled up to I\+Query\+Translator\+Factory. Method Create\+Query\+Translators accepting string as first argument marked as Obsolete. $\ast$ I\+Query\+Expression.\+Translate now has second boolean argument \textquotesingle{}filter\textquotesingle{} $\ast$ Added several methods which accepts I\+Query\+Expression to I\+Session\+Implementor, which is duplicating methods which accepts string. $\ast$ Miss-\/spelled Ado\+Net\+With\+Distrubted\+Transaction\+Factory removed\+: Use Ado\+Net\+With\+Distributed\+Transaction\+Factory instead $\ast$ Hql\+Distinct\+Holder removed\+: Use Hql\+Expression\+Sub\+Tree\+Holder instead $\ast$ Disable\+Log\+Formatted\+Sql \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} removed\+: the default is disabled $\ast$ I\+Session.\+Save\+Or\+Update\+Copy removed\+: Use Merge instead $\ast$ Oracle \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} My\+S\+Q\+L\+: The atan2 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} power \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a6ebc3cd8aa99ab15e71701961702fcfc}{functions}} now return double (instead of single) for consistency \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} other dialects. $\ast$ Removed Firebird\+Driver. It was the same as Firebird\+Client\+Driver since 3.\+2, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} the latter have been the default since then. $\ast$ Removed bunch of unused methods \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} $\ast$Helper classes $\ast$ Static fields \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a3a09c912178e06d15053fd07b1c9c94f}{on}} N\+Hibernate\+Util are declared as their exact class From N\+H4.\+0.\+0.\+Alpha1 to 4.\+0.\+0.Alpha2\+: Fixed \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_af263656e326663acf69eaf267b5b2798}{mapping}} by \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_afa2765f9f647ea2e9c46055f93a44d41}{code}} behaviour when map child subclasses (see NH-\/3135 \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} NH-\/3269) The constructor of Abstract\+Component\+Tuplizer now behaves like Abstract\+Entity\+Tuplizer \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the way \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} doesn\textquotesingle{}t create the instantiator any more. Custom component tuplizers \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a5d452122c551e70f3c0e36813a608148}{that}} derive directly from Abstract\+Component\+Tuplizer need to add this line of \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_afa2765f9f647ea2e9c46055f93a44d41}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} their constructor\+: instantiator = Build\+Instantiator(component)}

(hibernate.\+command\+\_\+timeout). -\/ Added named S\+QL query support. -\/ Allow to specify an \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a64e2bd2713b498c2d91c16de886df3fe}{isolation}} level when \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} (1.\+1.\+5). -\/ Upgraded log4net \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a35643e6cde36e0e5b6d5516664e8c947}{library}} to the latest \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a12136ab41a8aa67f0858137868a55106}{version}} (1.\+2.\+9). -\/ Fixed bug \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} Get/Load loading wrong subclasses because of class discriminant not being included \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} the generated query (Alexander Popov). -\/ Fixed Version\+Negative unsaved-\/value strategy not to treat 0 as the unsaved value. -\/ Fixed bug \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} Schema\+Export for a many-\/to-\/many relationship, \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a76868a71f10b10fd75a76f81ad936660}{it}} now generates a \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a48e7535f720104b60a6d6683444cd682}{table}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} non-\/null columns \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} a primary key. -\/ Added Increment\+Generator (Mark Holden). -\/ Fixed bug \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} $<$discriminator$>$ default value. -\/ Fixed bug \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_ad2bb08e650c6d8fdb35ccc26e9c0285e}{in}} proxy Equals \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a59a31db1436d75d219a8e2d9b645b3e0}{method}} always \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a0d55fd3715b114917fa9355fa820d8b8}{either}} returning true \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a94a8f61fe2f71cd81aac2f714ef26280}{or}} failing \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8releasenotes_8txt_a90786e910253733b32b96bd3e2fa613d}{with}} a N\+P\+E. -\/ Changed Lazy\+Initializer to match Hibernate 2.\+1, proxies now don\textquotesingle{}t have their own special implementation of Equals \mbox{\hyperlink{_n_hibernate_8license_8txt_a0ae30037179743e2ec49d709cd3e7bbb}{and}} Get\+Hash\+Code, \mbox{\hyperlink{_system_8_value_tuple_84_85_80_2_t_h_i_r_d-_p_a_r_t_y-_n_o_t_i_c_e_s_8_t_x_t_a0d55fd3715b114917fa9355fa820d8b8}{either}} System.\+Object\textquotesingle{}s
